${{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j$ = spatial background metric
${{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j$ = difference of spatial metric and spatial background metric
${{{ \gamma} _i} _j} = {{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} + {{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j}}$ = spatial metric

${{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = spatial background metric derivative
${{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = difference of spatial metric derivative and spatial background metric derivative, hyperbolic state variable
${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = spatial metric derivative
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$

${{{ b} ^i} _j} = {{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}}$
${{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}} = {{{ b} ^i} _j}$

connections:
${{{{ \Gamma} _i} _j} _k} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{\left({{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \gamma} _i} _k} _{,j}}{-{{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,i}}}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \Gamma} _i} _k} _j} + {{{{ \Gamma} _j} _k} _i}}$

${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{\frac{1}{2}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,m}}} + {{{{ \gamma} _m} _k} _{,j}} + {{{{ \gamma} _m} _j} _{,k}}}\right)}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$
${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ d} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ d} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{ d} _k} _m} _j}}\right)}}}$
using ${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$
${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ \hat{d}} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _m} _j} + {{{{ \hat{d}} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _j} _m} _k}{-{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _m} _j}}\right)}}}$

metric inverse partial:
${{\left( {{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}\right)} _{,k}} = {0}$
${{{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i} _{,k}}}}} = {0}$
${{{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i} _{,k}}}}} = {0}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _m} _{,k}}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ d} _k} _l} _m}}}}$
using ${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _l} _m} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _l} _m}}\right)}}}}$

$\alpha$ = lapse

lapse derivative:
${{ a} _i} = {{\left( \log\left( \alpha\right)\right)} _{,i}}$
${{ a} _i} = {{\frac{1}{\alpha}} {{ \alpha} _{,i}}}$
${{ \alpha} _{,i}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}}}$

lapse evolution:
${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{{{ \alpha} _{,i}}} {{{ \beta} ^i}}}{-{{{{\alpha}^{2}}} {{f}} {{\left({{K}{-{{{2}} {{\Theta}}}}}\right)}}}}}$
using ${{ \alpha} _{,i}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}}}$
${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{-{{{K}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}}\right)}}}$

lapse partial evolution
${{ { \alpha} _{,t}} _{,k}} = {{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{-{{{K}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}$
using ${{{ \alpha} _{,t}} _{,k}} = {{ { \alpha} _{,k}} _{,t}}$ ; ${{ \alpha} _{,i}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}}}$
${{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ a} _k} _{,t}}}} + {{{{ \alpha} _{,t}}} {{{ a} _k}}}} = {{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{-{{{K}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}$
using on lhs only ${{ a} _k} = {{\frac{1}{\alpha}} {{ \alpha} _{,k}}}$
${{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ a} _k} _{,t}}}} + {{{{ \alpha} _{,t}}} {{{\frac{1}{\alpha}} {{ \alpha} _{,k}}}}}} = {{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{-{{{K}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}$
subtracting ${{{ \alpha} _{,t}}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{\frac{1}{\alpha}}}$ from both sides
${{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ a} _k} _{,t}}}} = {{{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{-{{{K}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{{{ \alpha} _{,t}}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{\frac{1}{\alpha}}}}}}$
using ${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{-{{{K}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}}\right)}}}$
${{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ a} _k} _{,t}}}} = {{{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{-{{{K}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{\frac{1}{\alpha}}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{-{{{K}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}}\right)}}}}}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{\left( {{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}}{-{{{K}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}\right)} _{,k}}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{{\left( {{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}}{-{{{K}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}\right)} _{,k}} + {{\left( {{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{ a} _k}}\right)} _{,m}}{-{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{{ a} _k} _{,m}}}} + {{{{ a} _k}} {{b}}}}\right)}}{-{{\left( {{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{ a} _m}}\right)} _{,k}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{{ a} _m} _{,k}}}} + {{{{ a} _m}} {{{{ b} ^m} _k}}}}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{-{{\left( {{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{ a} _m}}\right)} _{,k}}} + {{\left( {{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{ a} _k}}\right)} _{,m}} + {{\left( {{{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{ a} _m}}}{-{{{K}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{{b}} {{{ a} _k}}}} + {{{{ a} _m}} {{{{ b} ^m} _k}}}}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{{\left( {{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{ a} _k}}\right)} _{,m}} + {{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{\left({{-{K}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{{b}} {{{ a} _k}}}} + {{{{ a} _m}} {{{{ b} ^m} _k}}}}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{{\left( {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{\left({{-{K}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}}}}\right)}} {{{{ δ} ^r} _k}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^r}} {{{ a} _k}}}\right)} _{,r}}{-{{{b}} {{{ a} _k}}}} + {{{{ a} _m}} {{{{ b} ^m} _k}}}}$

${{ a} _k} _{,t}$ source term: ${-{{{b}} {{{ a} _k}}}} + {{{{ a} _m}} {{{{ b} ^m} _k}}}$

metric evolution:
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{{{{-2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}} + {{{ \beta} _i} _{,j}} + {{{ \beta} _j} _{,i}}}{-{{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} _k} _i} _j}}}}}$

${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \gamma} _i} _k} _{,j}}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,i}}}}{-{{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \gamma} _k} _j} _{,i}}}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}{-{{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \gamma} _k} _i} _{,j}}}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^k} _{,j}}} {{{{ \gamma} _i} _k}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^k} _{,i}}} {{{{ \gamma} _j} _k}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}}}$
symmetrizing ${{ \gamma} _i} _j$

${{\frac{1}{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,t}} _{,k}}} = {{\left( {\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{{{-1}} {{{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j}}}}} + {{{ b} _i} _j} + {{{ b} _j} _i} + {{{-2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _l} _i} _j}}}}\right)}\right)} _{,k}}$

${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{\left( {\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{{{-1}} \cdot {{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j}}} + {{{ b} _i} _j} + {{{ b} _j} _i} + {{{-2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _l} _i} _j}}}}\right)}\right)} _{,k}}$
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{{\left( {\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{{{-1}} \cdot {{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j}}} + {{{ b} _i} _j} + {{{ b} _j} _i} + {{{-2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _l} _i} _j}}}}\right)}\right)} _{,k}} + {{\left( {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}\right)} _{,l}}{-{\left({{{{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,l}}}} + {{{b}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}}\right)}}{-{{\left( {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}\right)} _{,k}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,l}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}}}$
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{-{{\left( {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}\right)} _{,k}}} + {{\left( {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}\right)} _{,l}} + {{\left( {\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{{{ b} _j} _i} + {{{ b} _i} _j}{-{{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j}}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _l} _i} _j}}}}\right)}\right)} _{,k}}{-{{{b}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}}}$
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{{\left( {-{{{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}}} + {{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{{{ b} _j} _i} + {{{ b} _i} _j}{-{{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j}}}}{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _l} _i} _j}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}} + {{-{{{b}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}}} + {{\left( {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}\right)} _{,l}}}$

Riemann curvature
${{{{{ R} ^i} _j} _k} _l} = {{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _l} _{,k}}{-{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} _{,l}}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _l}}}}{-{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _l}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _k}}}}}$

Ricci curvature
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{{{{ R} ^k} _i} _k} _j}$
using ${{{{{ R} ^k} _i} _k} _j} = {{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _i} _j} _{,k}}{-{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _i} _k} _{,j}}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _m} _k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _i} _j}}}}{-{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _m} _j}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _i} _k}}}}}$

Z4 $\Theta$ definition
${{ \Theta} _{,t}} = {{{{\left( {{\Theta}} \cdot {{{ \beta} ^k}}\right)} _{,k}} + {{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ Z} ^k}}\right)} _{,k}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{R}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{ d} ^k}{-{{{2}} {{{ a} ^k}}}}}\right)}} {{{ Z} _k}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{K}} {{\left({{K}{-{{{2}} {{\Theta}}}}}\right)}}}{-{{{{{ K} ^m} _n}} {{{{ K} ^n} _m}}}}{-{{{16}} {{π}} \cdot {{\rho}}}}}\right)}}}}{-{{{\Theta}} \cdot {{b}}}}}$
using the definition of R

		(deriv)->Z_l.x += Z_l.x * b_ul.x.x + Z_l.z * b_ul.z.x + Z_l.y * b_ul.y.x;
		(deriv)->Z_l.y += Z_l.x * b_ul.x.y + Z_l.z * b_ul.z.y + Z_l.y * b_ul.y.y;
		(deriv)->Z_l.z += Z_l.x * b_ul.x.z + Z_l.z * b_ul.z.z + Z_l.y * b_ul.y.z;
		(deriv)->beta_u.x += beta_u.x * b_ul.x.x + beta_u.y * b_ul.x.y + beta_u.z * b_ul.x.z + -a_u.x * tmp1 + 2. * e_u.x * tmp1 + -d_u.x * tmp1;
		(deriv)->beta_u.y += beta_u.x * b_ul.y.x + beta_u.y * b_ul.y.y + beta_u.z * b_ul.y.z + -a_u.y * tmp1 + 2. * e_u.y * tmp1 + -d_u.y * tmp1;
		(deriv)->beta_u.z += beta_u.x * b_ul.z.x + beta_u.y * b_ul.z.y + beta_u.z * b_ul.z.z + -a_u.z * tmp1 + 2. * e_u.z * tmp1 + -d_u.z * tmp1;
	}
	<? end ?>/* useShift == "2005 Bona / 2008 Yano" */
